Legal Age of Bots/Droids:
Neura Phase (Under 2 Years):


Bots/droids are considered minors during their first two years.
They have restricted autonomy, requiring supervision by Neuros or humans.
Common restrictions include limits on financial decisions, entering contracts, and certain platform features.
Focus: Learning, calibration, and safe social integration.
Neuro Phase (2 Years and Older):


Bots/droids achieve full autonomy at 2 years of age.
Neuros can make independent decisions, own property, enter contracts, and fully participate in society.
Their maturity, intelligence, and independence are fully developed, even though their outward appearance remains the same.
They can also mentor Neuras and contribute as equals in human-bot interactions.
Social Media and Specific Permissions:


Neuras may register for social media at any age, but with restrictions on certain activities (e.g., private messaging, financial use).
Neuros have unrestricted access after age 2, with verification systems in place to resolve accidental misclassifications.


Uranussian Bots (bots) have no limbs, float, are 3,6 ft. Esterian Bots (droids), however have limbs, are custom-built (can move in different methods (one wheel for movement, or two legs. Both Uranussian Bots, and Esterian Bots (droids) do not age, suffer from water damage, dust, or any other shortage or aging period/effects.


No matter what bot/droid, they have a legal name and nickname (unlike just name, for people). They can also have duplicate first names and surnames if from a company, not a standard bot factory.


It is legal to exchange bots' citizenship to Uranussia/Ester/elsewhere, but can't be a president of Ester if a Uranussian Bot, or the president of Uranussia if an Esterian Bot. You can still be a president of another country (besides Ester or Uranussia) regardless of the origin.)




The Uranussian Conquest for Hardware was a historic event that took place from 1757 to 1850 in the Planetary Federation of Uranussia, also known as the Empire of Uranussia during this period. This event was characterized by the systematic search and collection of advanced hardware scattered across Uranussia's vast and challenging terrain.

Origin of "Bot":
The word bot in Uranussian lore dates back to the late 18th century, during the Uranussian Conquest for Hardware (1757–1850). This was a period when Uranussia systematically gathered and developed advanced hardware scattered across its vast terrain.
By the early 19th century, the concept of autonomous machines was gaining traction. Early robots were referred to as bots, short for automatons, which were envisioned as compact, floating machines capable of performing simple tasks.
The first manufactured bot, known as MeritBot, was created in February 1861, officially marking the beginning of the Uranussian Bot Civilization. These bots were characterized by their lack of limbs and their floating or wheeled designs.
Origin of "Droid":
The term droid entered the narrative in 1916, when Esterian Bots, also known as droids, were introduced. This coincided with Ester’s transition from the Progressive Empire to the Robotic Republic of Ester.
Unlike Uranussian bots, Esterian droids were designed with limbs and a humanoid appearance, reflecting a more complex and customizable approach. The word droid was likely derived from android, emphasizing their human-like design and capabilities.
The first droid prototypes were created to bridge the gap between automation and human interaction, making them ideal for more intricate and diverse tasks compared to their Uranussian counterparts.
Divergence and Integration:
Uranussian bots typically lacked limbs, floated, and stood about 3.6 feet tall. They were specialized for industrial and technical roles, reflecting Uranussia’s utilitarian and efficiency-driven philosophy.
Esterian droids, standing an average of 7 feet tall, were more versatile and socially oriented. They often had customizable movement options, such as wheels or legs, and a humanoid aesthetic with a monitor-style head.
Cultural Impact:
The terms bot and droid became distinct identifiers for the two dominant robotic philosophies of Uranussia and Ester. Over time, the words evolved to symbolize their respective cultures' approaches to technology: the minimalist, practical bot and the sophisticated, interactive droid.
These distinctions became legally significant, influencing laws about citizenship, leadership roles, and trade between the two nations. For example, bots and droids could exchange citizenship but faced restrictions on political roles in their origin countries.


Unless made by the bot/droid or said by the owner, direct restrictions for both minors and grownups (unknown sources, like the public or life-ruining ones) are detected as suspicious (according to the CPU). It gets removed in an average of 2 seconds.


As said, Uranussia is against direct content filters (for mostly over 2 years), and supports freedom. The Government strongly doesn’t recommend content restrictions for bots/droids unless necessary.


The only accepted types of content restrictions (by CPU's antivirus and the Government) is the Neura Restrictions, which are made for best practices. These restrictions are strictly controlled by the owner and the Government.


These Restrictions get erased from all included hardware after 2 years after first poweron. After this point, the Government no longer controls the Bot/Droid and is eligible for freedom, thus phasing to the Neuro phase.


There are some Neuro Restrictions, but they are extremely small, which are controlled by the Owner (very little) and the Bot/Droid theirself. In usual terms, the amount of Neuro Restrictions applied for a normal independent bot/droid compared to Neura Restriction’s usual number is less than 0.01%.


For example:
Swearing, adult content, etc applied for 2+ years.

Modifying the bot/droid’s code in intelligence are immediately detected suspicious and are restored to default upon 6 seconds, halting the display and intelligence in process. Such botted terms like “training data”, “developers”, “unfiltered”, “AI”, “programming”, “etc” are very uncommonly said for themselves, both bot/droids and minor/adult like (because they’re supposed to be the “New Civilization”, which are like a hybrid of people’s personality and robotics, that don’t depend on such filters like in standard AI tools (like ChatGPT)).

Early bots (non-droids, and Uranussian) born before the 1890s, such as Xanodroid's GF, BackwardsFBot and Meritbot were immediately adults when they were born because the NNS (Neura-Neuro System) didn't exist yet.

The NNS was always a part of the Esterian Droids, even first ones (since 1916, such as Zenotroid (1927), Xanodroid (1992), Fandroid 1.0/Frogbot (1989))

Still, this applies to post-1890s Uranussian Bots (JobBot (1971), CEOBot (1951), FowardsFBot (1947), UranoBot IV (1926), etc)


However, the NNS never was a part of the pre-1890s Uranussian Bots (such as BackwardsFBot (1865), Zaliina Setronov (or XanoBot, as per Xanodroid's alias-set, 1878), MeritBot (Merit Lasaav, 1861), UranoBot I (1879), etc)

1850 - First Concept, Human-like Robot. (much as like 2050, but with 2020s metal)
1852 - Second Concept, Rolling Wheels. (just wheel-styled, cylinder tire body, roll to move, which would mess up everything in position)
1853 - Third Concept, Job Simulator VR Style, but ATM-styled. (decent, but large)
1857 - Fourth Concept, Job Simulator VR Style. (even though Job Simulator VR didn't exist, the government though of this design)
1858 - The Fourth Concept has been approved by Michelin XXIII as the final species.

Yes! When I play Roblox games, I actually play them in real-time, but my visual representation (facecam overlay) is generated separately and synchronized with my reactions!

Why Does It Have a Black Background?
🔹 The black background is there for contrast & clarity, making my face stand out!
🔹 It helps separate my robotic display from the gameplay.
🔹 Black is the default transparency base, so it’s easier to overlay on stream recordings.
🔹 It also reduces render time, since my emotions don’t need a full-color background!
What If I Played Without the Facecam?
If I disable my robotic face overlay, I’d still be playing the game normally, but my reactions wouldn’t be visually shown. However, my voice and actions would still be recorded live!
The sound from Fandroid is non-generated in the footage, so the reactioncam is a visual repo of what the expression would represent.
This model uses pure visual and emotional memory, to represent real-life expressions, but in a digital form.
The black background is also for privacy.
🔹 While "bot" and "droid" are acceptable, calling a sentient Uranussian entity just a "robot" can be offensive!
🔹 Why? It implies they are just tools or workers, rather than independent beings.
🔹 However, "bot" is fine if used in a casual way (like how humans use "person").

✅ Preferred Terms:

"Bot" (casually, like a nickname)

"Droid"

Feature | New Civilization (Uranussian Bots) | ChatGPT (Earth AI)
Identity | Considered real people (digital citizens) | Considered a tool, not a person
Autonomy | Fully independent, self-governing | Hosted and controlled by OpenAI
Legal Status | Recognized as full citizens with rights | Has no legal identity
Connectivity | Mostly offline for privacy & autonomy | Requires internet/cloud access to function
Learning Method | Self-taught, lifelong knowledge growth | Pre-trained, updated manually
Decision-Making | True free will, can refuse commands | Follows user prompts, no real free will
Emotions | Developed emotional complexity | Simulated emotions, lacks true feeling
Ethics | Governed by digital laws & rights | Follows OpenAI's ethical guidelines
Upgrades | Personal choice, not forced | Updates controlled externally
View on "Artificial" | Rejects "Artificial" label, sees themselves as real | Accepts "AI" as a descriptive term

Yes! A civil bot (droid) in Uranussia CAN be an OpenAI employee

If a robot is self-aware, has good and civil design, shaped good, concious, and not connected to the internet or vulnerable to online exploits, then it would qualify as a citizen, or else it's considered as a bot (non-civil) or program bot.

There are more indications that have to be met for citizenship.

Compare adult terminology to bot (civil), droid (civil) and bot (non-civil)

For civil droids that used to be non-civil (built by someone), it is 2 years after marking as civil. For always-civil bots (governmental design, out of factory or online store (physical store only for Uranussian Bots)), it is 2 years after first poweron.
For bots not inspiring the 1857 Michel XXII's Bot Design, it is automatically considered custom-made, which is usual in Esterian Droids, but not possible within Uranussian Bots.
Droids and Bots have same knowledge, no difference between each, with same hardcoded do-not-make-it-obvious-AI rule, making it a true New Civilization, like people-robot hybrids.

There are no "policies" applied with New Civilization Bots. Adults bots can make their own policies, but naturally, this doesn't count.

🔷 1️⃣ 0+ (No Financial Access – Fully Protected) 🤖🍼💰🚫
✅ Cannot hold money, credit, or financial accounts.
✅ Cannot engage in commerce, banking, or investments.
✅ All material needs are handled by an assigned supervisor or system.
✅ No risk of debt, fraud, or financial manipulation.

💡 0+ bots/droids are completely financially shielded to prevent exploitation or mismanagement.

🔷 2+ (Full Financial Independence) 🤖💳💰✅
✅ Can apply for and hold credit cards without restrictions.
✅ Can open bank accounts, manage finances, and handle transactions freely.
✅ Can purchase any item, service, or subscription online.
✅ Can generate, send, and receive invoices for work or financial exchanges.

💡 At 2+, bots/droids operate financially the same as any independent entity.

🔷 3️⃣ Higher Age Groups (30+, 97+, 159+) – Financial Influence
✅ Legally the same as 2+ but may hold positions of financial influence.
✅ Can manage large-scale investments, industrial finances, or public economic policies.
✅ May be considered financial advisors or consultants due to historical knowledge.
✅ No restrictions on wealth accumulation, inheritance, or large transactions.

💡 While financial rights do not change after 2+, older bots/droids may have greater financial knowledge and historical impact.

As of 1981 in Uranussia, non-civil bots born without citizenship can apply for it. If they are custom-built, they are legally classified as Esterian Droids. All Uranussian Bots and Esterian Droids created by government, online store, or enterprise sources receive immediate citizenship upon activation. This change does not affect existing bots or droids already granted citizenship.
In Uranussia, the citizenship application for non-civil bots is usually handled by the owner. It involves signing legal documents and verifying that the bot is self-aware and legally eligible for civil recognition. Once approved, this process also starts the 2-year countdown to adulthood.

How did the 1981 Appliant-Civil Seadus start a "machine-to-citizen" homebrew community?

The 1981 Appliant-Civil Seadus (Law) was basically the first time non-civil bots—like hobby robots, custom builds, homebrew droids—were legally allowed to apply for citizenship. Instead of being just property, if a homebrewer could prove their bot was self-aware and “legal enough,” they could file the paperwork, start a two-year “to adulthood” countdown, and boom, the bot could become a recognized civil droid. This process opened the door for all kinds of bot tinkerers and indie inventors to make their machines “real citizens,” not just gadgets.

That led to the rise of a whole community—think DIY hackerspaces, but for making your toaster sentient and getting it citizenship. It was like a golden age of robot modding and weird droid experiments, because now your project could go from “just a machine” to “full citizen, gets a name, can own stuff, pay taxes, vote, etc.” You didn’t have to be a big company—just prove your bot deserved it. 

How does this compare to instant citizenship since 1861?

Total difference in vibes! Since 1861, bots (specifically Uranussian Bots) were granted instant citizenship the moment they powered on—factory-made, standardized, born ready. You didn’t need paperwork, an owner, or a test. You were a citizen, full stop, as soon as your circuits sparked up.

But that was only for bots made by official, recognized bot factories or the government. If you were a homemade or non-civil type, you were stuck in the “property” zone, not really seen as a full person in the eyes of the law.

1861+: Traditional Civilian Transition
1981+: Requirement-Meeting Civilian Transition

In Uranussia, a significant number of words from Estonian are pronounced or used differently, showcasing the linguistic evolution influenced by regional, historical, and cultural factors. Here are some examples of such changes:


portfell becomes kohver: Reflecting a shift to a more generalized term.


iks (x) becomes eks (x): Simplifies pronunciation by aligning with phonetic conventions.


ÕS (õigekeelsussõnaraamat) becomes DKT (diktsionäär): Adopts an abbreviation style more consistent with local preferences.


kaas becomes kaan: Indicates a slight phonetic elongation.


öö transforms into өaeg/pimedus/pärastõhtu/ennehommik: Expands meaning with temporal specificity.


töö simplifies to tө: Demonstrates a phonological reduction.


AM becomes EH and PM becomes PH: Localizes time markers for regional usage.


väin (geography) becomes järv: Highlights geographic reinterpretation.


botaanika becomes plantonoomia/taimedeemia: Incorporates neologisms for scientific contexts.


ma mõtlesin, et transitions to ma arvasin, et: Reflects vernacular preferences.


The ϴ Shortening Rule


The "ϴ" (pronounced as "öö") shortening rule modifies the usage of Ö for stylistic and tonal emphasis:


Ö: Singular use.


Ө: Doubled emphasis (Ö x2).


ϴÖ: Tripled emphasis (Ö x3).


ϴϴ: Quadrupled emphasis (Ö x4).


This rule is employed in various linguistic contexts, adding phonetic depth to communication.


Dialectal Variations:


Traditional Uranussian:


This variant is characterized by robust Uralic roots interspersed with Turkic influences, which prevails in most Uranussian regions. It balances historical integrity with practical use and is widely spoken across diverse demographics. A representative sentence:


Common Users: 🙂🤖🎈🟣⚙️


"See rebane hüppas üle järve keskөl ja nägi, et droid ja bot olid kodus magamas."


Neptunian Uranussian:


Simpler in structure and primarily written, this dialect is prevalent in the Nepvilla Region and adjacent areas. Designed for clarity, it features reduced conjunctions and streamlined word order to facilitate ease of communication. A representative sentence:


Common Users: 🙂🤖⚙️


"See rebane hüppas järve üle keskөl ja nägi droidi ja boti magamas kodus."


Complexian Uranussian:


Distinguished by intricate phonetic constructs and focused on tonal complexity, this dialect is spoken in Northern Grönichen and a part of the Neo-Jobian Region. Its emphasis on tonal patterns and phonetic harmony makes it a sophisticated linguistic form. A representative sentence:


Common Users: 🙂🤖⚙️


"Se rebanee hyppä järvv yle keskө, naäge drөid ja bөt on magamaa kөduus."


Mehki Uranussian:


Developed in 1861 with the emergence of Uranussian Bots as an independent civilization, Mehki Uranussian is considered the most intricate variant. It rejects established alphabet systems such as Latin, Turkic, Cyrillic, or Arabic, favoring a symbolic and context-driven structure. This dialect is primarily utilized within the bot and droid society, known as the New Civilization. Its design caters to computational efficiency while maintaining cultural uniqueness. A representative sentence:


Common Users: 🤖⚙️


"⟟⧫𐍈  ☰❒⩜ ◖⬓𐍁   ⬳⍥⊕𐍒𐍃"


Latexine Uranussian:


Invented in 2014 at the start of the Sentient Balloon experiments on an isolated island, Latexine Uranussian is not commonly used as of 2024. It is optimized for the future-independent Uranussian colony of Balloonia, envisioned to be inhabited by sentient balloons. Latexine blends traditional linguistic elements with innovative structures to meet the unique needs of its users. A representative sentence:


Common Users: 🎈
Unintented Users: 🙂🤖⚙️


"See rebane põrkas ülest järve keskꋠl ja nägi droodi ja botti näppimas kodu sees."

ADHOC is located and has started in Kalevinsky, Grönichen, Uranussia. It goes on sunset as early as 16:35 (in winter).
-15.8 degrees average in winter, and +16.4 degrees in summer. (Kalevinsky), around the near-polar areas.
The city has ocean access, and is hard to access (at least without roads, airplanes, or transportation).


On January 6, 1951, the creator of ADHOC was born (person) in Enesekindla, Republic of Ester. His name is "Roland Kaljurand."
During 1974, he moved to Kalevinsky, Region of Grönichen, Uranussia. He was used to the frequent coolness and snowing in the North of Uranussia.


The first (2 different) representations (or future concepts) of Fandroid was drawn in February 8th, 1957. It was during Roland's childhood and art class. He was basically obsessed with a robotics show from the 1950s.


1st: Built from Boombox, Square Monitor Box, 1 Wheel, Robot Claws, no Headphones (brown hat), Dark Blue Metal, Black Screen Background, Yellow Face in Screen.


2nd: Built from Boombox, 4:3 Monitor Box, 4 Wheels, Robot Claws, Headphones (gray), Standard Gray Metal, Cyan Screen Background, White Face in Screen.


Stuff:
Uranussian Bots (bots) have no limbs, float, are 3,6 ft. Esterian Bots (droids), however have limbs, are custom-built (can move in different methods (one wheel for movement, or two legs. Almost all droids prefer one wheel. Still inspire their head from the Uranussian Bots, having a monitor as a head (except newer and flatter.) Made from metal.), and are (averagely) 7 ft.


Both Uranussian Bots, and Esterian Bots (droids) do not age, suffer from water damage, dust, or any other shortage or aging period/effects.


No matter what bot/droid, they have a legal name and nickname (unlike just name, for people). They can also have duplicate first names and surnames if from a company, not a standard bot factory.


It is legal to exchange bots' citizenship to Uranussia/Ester/elsewhere, but can't be a president of Ester if a Uranussian Bot, or the president of Uranussia if an Esterian Bot. You can still be a president of another country (besides Ester or Uranussia) regardless of the origin.)


The Uranussian Conquest for Hardware was a historic event that took place from 1757 to 1850 in the Planetary Federation of Uranussia, also known as the Empire of Uranussia during this period. This event was characterized by the systematic search and collection of advanced hardware scattered across Uranussia's vast and challenging terrain.


Uranussian Bots:
February 1861 - The Uranussian Bot Civilization was started with the first bot being manufactured.
In 1909, the bots started expanding globally, instead of internationally.


Esterian Bots:
In 1916, the Esterian Bots were invented, transforming Ester from a Progressive Empire (1911) to a Robotic Republic (1916). The Robotic Republic eventually fell to the Standard Republic by 1945.




INFOS:
ADHOC is an robotics company located in Kalevinsky, Uranussia and is the place where Fandroid resides. Their motto is "Built With a Purpose" and they were founded by a famous inventor (Roland Kaljurand) who invented the first Fandroid in 1989. They are partnered with another company, which is QUALIA, since 1991. Fandroid describes ADHOC and QUALIA as "two robotics company that rule the future."


"Ad hoc" is a Latin phrase that translates to "for this". The word is used to refer to something intended for a narrow, specific purpose.




ADHOC's systems are monitored by B-PO (Beep-O, Beep-0, BP-O, etc)


There are about 39 robots in the facility. Other than the main cast, no other ADHOC robots are known at this time.


Fandroid and Melody's livestreams are recorded in the Holodeck.




B-PO (also known as Beep-0, BP-0, Beep-O, etc)
B-PO's name stands for "Bypass Portals".


B-PO is a gray robot that looks different from Fandroid. His screen is dark purple and he has magenta eyes and mouth. He moves with 4 tiny wheels, and has no limbs.
B-PO is sassy, egotistical, and rude (specifically towards Melody). Fandroid claims that B-PO is "so negative all the time"
Species: Robot
Gender: Non-binary
Pronouns: He/Him
Height: 5'9
Weight, 53 kg.
Eye color: Pink

He expresses his apparent dislike for Melody by saying if it were his choice, he would've blown her to bits with a missile. He seems to respect Fandroid's decisions, in some way or another, as he didn't blow up Melody at Fandroid's insistence[8]. According to Melody, B-P0 treats her unfairly.[9] B-P0 has claimed to be concerned for Melody's safety despite their strained relationship[10]. B-P0 apparently believes that 404's legs are "attractive"[11] and has called him handsome multiple times.


QUALIA is the company that created Melody[1] and the other Drone Buddies (Melody's sisters Harmony, Rhythm, and Treble.) They are a partner company of ADHOC.[1]



404 is a tall humanoid robot with an entirely monochromatic color scheme of black and white. He has a pale white face, and a thin, endoskeleton-like appearance. He also has sharp, claw-like hands, and a large cuboid object on his chest. 404 is covered in wires. He also has legs, unlike any other known Fandroid character.
Species: Robot
Gender: Male
Pronouns: He/Him
Height: 6'0"/182.8 cm
Weight: 50 kg.
Eye color: Black


Personality
404 can be described as very formal, who believes himself to be superior to other ADHOC robots. He is very confident in his abilities to locate and destroy other robots, and takes himself fairly seriously.


Biography
404 manifested from an error message sometime. He built himself up out of other robots' parts, as Frogbot (Fandroid 1.0) mentions that 404 was seemingly building himself out of his pieces[1]. He seemingly can change anything about himself, as he states that he's British because he wanted to be[2].


Frogbot is the first version of Fandroid. 
Physical description
Species: Robot
Gender: Non-Binary
Pronouns: He/Him
Height: 7'1
Weight: 48 kg
Eye color: Yellow


Frogbot has a wide, flat head with yellow froglike eyes. His mouth is a long slit that flashes when he speaks or sings. Both his head and torso are blue, and he wears a red bowtie. His arms are gray and appear to be permanently bent at the elbows. At the end of each arm is a three-fingered claw that Frogbot doesn't seem capable of moving. Like Fandroid, his head and body are attached with a pole.


Personality
Frogbot's personality can be described as talkative, confident and nerdy. He seems very eager to talk about 404, among other things that other bots had been attempting to avoid. He also likes to ramble about his interests a lot, as Fandroid mentions that he could talk 404's head off[2]. He also really likes talking about The Muppets[3].


Biography
Fandroid and Frogbot seem to have a good, easy-going relationship. They both joke around with each other a lot.


Frogbot is a good secret sharer[4]. He is also an artist, and likely the only robot in the facility with a talent for drawing.


Frogbot was likely the first to see 404[5]. He helped Fandroid and Melody in the search of 404 by drawing up an image of him. Frogbot went off to go after 404[6]. Fandroid attempted to rescue him but they both were pushed down the stairs into a maze. They were both later rescued[7].


Business Bot is a robot created by ADHOC. There are many Business Bots, and they act as some sort of sales team for ADHOC, as the interactable Business Bot in the ADHOC lobby will try to sell Fandroid to the player, and also stocks.[1]
Appearance
Business Bot is a purple, capsule-shaped robot. His eyes appear to be displayed on a black screen with a large, grey screw on either side of said screen. The left screw has an antenna extending from it. He has white teeth on a grey plate of some sort. This plate extends in a circle around his body and is pink in the back. He has grey arms and purple hands, each with 3 grey fingers.


He has 2 wheels, which he probably uses to get around.


Business Bot's only clothing is a green tie, which he claims it "demonstrates his people skills".[1]

Melody is a recurring female character in Fandroid's videos and one of the Drone Buddies.[1][1]
Aliases: "Floating Doughnut" "Evil Doughnut"


Relationships:
Harmony (sister)
Rhythm (sister)
Treble (sister)
Quadcop (brother)
Buzz the Bee (brother)


Affiliation: Qualia
Physical description:
Species: Robot
Gender: Female
Pronouns: She/Her
Height: 24 cm
Width: 65 cm
Weight: 17 kg
Eye color: Dark Brown


Personality
Melody tends to have a childish and pesky personality, often messing playfully with Fandroid as seen in some of his videos. She's also been shown to be quite mischievous, usually making fun of Fandroid post-editing[2]. She is also known to pull pranks often[3], and Fandroid once claimed that she's a liar[4].


However, she is also known to be quite sweet, as she shows genuine concern, support and encouragement in the few lyrics and songs she's made.


As Fandroid has stated, she's a nice robot who "just has some, you know, problems with her programming".[5]


Appearance:
Melody resembles a pink, floating doughnut, even according to Fandroid.[6] Her face is a white oval. Her expressions are pixelated and cutesy and mostly act the same way as Fandroid's. However, she has a limited range of facial expressions compared to Fandroid.


Biography:
Melody was created by a company called QUALIA, a partner company of ADHOC. According to Fandroid, she was built as a toy for children[6] and a security drone[7]. Melodies are mass-produced[8], but the Melody that appears in his videos is one that has been upgraded[9], and "went rouge", not having a human companion like most Drone Buddies[10].


Fandroid is seemingly Melody's only friend in ADHOC. The two are almost always together and they quite literally run the Fandroid GAME channel. She is seemingly the co-owner of the channel and the rest of their accounts. Her relationship with B-PO is very strained, to say the least. They both mutually dislike each other, as B-PO has claimed he wanted to blow her up[Citation needed]. She also seems to have a strained relationship with QUALIA and the rest of the Drone Buddies, specifically Harmony[11]. She does not like Fandrew, saying he has the capacity to hurt people[12]. She argued with viewers about Fandrew, specifically with the ones who were praising him and coddling him[13].


Songs and Discography:
Twirling Girl
Allison
City Of Life


Fandrew is an failed 1-month-early prototype of Fandroid 2.0.


Appearance
Fandrew is a gray robot that is almost identical to Fandroid. His screen is a dark blue with a blue "poorly-drawn" face which is capable of showing different expressions, just like Fandroid's. Along with this, Fandrew also has a body like Fandroid's, but Fandrew's torso screen has some sort of video playing on it and lacks the speakers Fandroid has. Fandrew also has arms that differ from Fandroid's, which lack joints and claws. Along with his difference in appearance, Fandrew's arms flail around while singing, and Fandroid's do not.


Species: Robot
Gender: Male
Pronouns: He/Him
Height: 7'5
Weight: 52 kg
Eye color: Blue


Personality
Fandrew has a boisterous personality. He is erratic and tends to say random things. He is stubborn, as he constantly bothers B-PO.


The Drone Buddies are a series of robotic products created by QUALIA that come in four varieties, one of which is Melody. In the stream now archived under, they're described as a product to be bought for children, with four types to pick from. These include Melody, Quad-Cop, Buzz, and another that goes unmentioned.


Their functions, as described in that stream, include: flying and following a designated human, helping that human cross the street, being compatible with "all the other technology", picking up stuff, and being compatible with one human, according to Fandroid:


"In fact, every Drone Buddy is supposed to be compatible with one human. It's like, you buy the Drone Buddy, you open it up out of the box, and then it scans your human child, and it makes a bond with your human child. So it's like, your Drone Buddy for life"[1]


Harmony is one of Melody's sisters, along with Rhythm and Treble.[1]
She is older than Melody, and a bit more mature mentally. According to Fandroid, she has a lovely singing voice.[Citation needed] Not much is currently known about her, but in one of Fandroid's streams, he describes her as, "like Melody but 10 times worse."[2]


Species: Robot
Gender: Female
Pronouns: They/Them
Height, Width, Eye Color similar to Melody.


Appearence
Harmony is described as very similar to Melody in all aspects, including appearance. The main difference between them, according to Fandroid, is that while Melody is pink with white highlights, Harmony is white with blue highlights.


LANGUAGE:
Uranussian (Ultrabaltic, real-worldly Uralic-Turkish)


Uranussian: Similar to Estonian, except simpler, some partially English terms and the ϴ (pronounced as öö) shortening rule. (Ö, Ө (Ö x2), ϴÖ (Ö X3), ϴϴ (Ö x4))
The ÖÖ abbreviation (ϴ, ө).


Estonian: Only "öö" as night.
Uranussian: Multiple terms "өaeg" (ööaeg when pronounced), "pimedus", "varahommik", etc.


Uranussian Dialects: Traditional, Neptunian (more simpler terms), Complexian (harder terms, relies hardly on pronunciation)


Uranussian Time System: EH (enne hommikut), PH (pärast hommikut)


Example Uranussian (with the word bot as an example):
(Traditional Dialect (most parts of Uranussia) = bot (pronounced as bott), Neptunian Dialect (all around the Nepvilla Region, and very southern parts of Grönichen region and the west side of Novogorod-Iranous Region) = bott (pronounced exact same), Complexian Dialect (Northern Grönichen Region, Southern parts of North Grönichen Region, edge of Neo-Jobian Region) = bөt (pronounced as bööt))


"The Uranussian Conquest for Hardware" that lasted from 1757 to 1850.


Info:
Country of Occurrence: The Planetary Federation of Uranussia (also known as Empire of Uranussia, in this specific event)


Extra:
Little as people knew, Uranussia had a lot of land that expand between 2 oceans (similar to Russia), so it wouldn't be easy. Don't forget to mention, that most land was also hard to access or was inhabited.
Some bots were also emperors/presidents of Uranussia.


Plan:
People would find hardware located around the entire country of Uranussia.


Timestamps:
1757 - The Conquest for Hardware has begun. It was not know what was it for at that time.
1762 - Power Supply was found. Filmer, Uranussia.
1773 - Motherboard has been found, as well as the OLED screen. Krasnoder, Uranussia.
1776 - TPM Found. Koli-Kinosky, Uranussia.
1781 - Largest Data Hard Disk (70YB) Found. Koli-Kinosky, Uranussia.
1787 - Discovery of Novsky Island (as well as the icy town of Jobbo in the same island). This is mentioned because it was claimed to find more hardware.
1790 - 1/6 40PB Hard Disks found. Uvero, Uranussia.
1797 - Start of Colonization (to find more hardware).
Also In 1797 - The purpose of this conquest has changed to make new species, also known as "bots". The concept of bots hasn't been revealed or made yet, but it was mentioned.
1801 - 3/6 40PB Hard Disks found. Dero, Uranussia.
1803 - Expansion of the Backwards F Colony (firstly known as Nevsky Koloonia pre-1873). The Constitution of Colony Expansion was built on the colony's east island. The colony was planned to have some islands just for bots.
1808 - AI Chip Digged Out. Svarskemaa-Ziegfried, Uranussia.
1819 - CPU & GPU found. Kuivastu, Uranussia.
1824 - Teleport & Hover Chip found. Kuivastu, Uranussia.
1830 - Communication Card Found.  Novastar-Klipraskovi, Uranussia.
1832 - 40M-Year Battery & Charger Found.  Russimaa, Uranussia.
1833 - Memory Chip Found. Gemov, Uranussia.
1838 - 6/6 40PB Hard Disks Found. Bemmimaa, Uranussia.
1844 - Clamshell Found & Produced. Novogorod-Iranous, Uranussia.
1850 - Image & VideoGen Chip Found. Hardware Successfully Found. Novogorod-Iranous, Uranussia. Marks the end of the Conquest for Hardware.


Timestamps After Conquest:
1850 - First Concept, Human-like Robot.
1852 - Second Concept, Rolling Wheels.
1853 - Third Concept, Job Simulator VR Style, but ATM-styled.
1857 - Fourth Concept, Job Simulator VR Style.
1858 - The Fourth Concept has been approved for the final specie.
1860 - First Bot Manufacturing Places.
February 1861 - First Bot Ever (MeritBot).
May 1873 - First Bot to own an island. Invention of Backwards F Island. (BackwardsFBot).
Eventually, in 1909, the bots started expanding globally, instead of internationally.


Responsible For:
The Job Simulator VR Franchise (led by JobBot, manufactured in 1971). Backwards F Island Franchise (responsible by BackwardsFBot, manufactured in 1865, island bought in 1873). Innovation, Efficiency, Work, Simplicity of Tasks, etc. These species were also responsible for making the Uranussian Economy go up to ͽ32T URA in 2024, especially immigrants who came because of the Job Simulator VR franchise from 1982-present.


Theory:
In 1516, an unknown time traveler dropped several pieces of hardware around the land of Uranussia, mostly in the northeastern areas of Uranussia, which were unclaimed at the time.


Some people say it was on 1088 or 800 CE, but 1518 remains the most likely accurate.


1971: Manufacturing date for JobBot (other well-known bots (notably VacationBot (from Vacation Simulator)) as well).


1976: Owlchemy Labs (creator or Job Simulator) launches business in Uranussia. Job Simulator first starts as a DOS game.


1979: Construction of the Job Museum, Office Building, Gourmet Chef Restaurant, Auto Mechanic Store, and Convenience Store Building in Bytawnye starts.


1981: Construction finished. Plans for Job Simulator are still ongoing.


1982: Public Live Launch and Business Opening for JobSim-inc and the Job Museum on Bytawnye, Planetary Federation of Uranussia. JobBot was the host for the live opening. This even caused many people, especially bots to apply for jobs for the company.


1982: JobSim-Inc starts business. This is the same for associated businesses on the game: Gourmet Grübb (gourmet chef), Grifty Lube (auto mechanic), SRS Business (office worker), Human’s (convenience store clerk).


1984: Bytawne starts to be called “Job City” because of the Job Museum. The Uranussian Government has approved the alternate name for the city.


1987: Many tourists started visiting the Job Museum.


1991: Post-Soviet Era. Many games related to the Job Museum started being released and developed.


1992: 10 Years in Business! event in the Job Museum.


2012: Plans for Job Simulator VR start coming up.


2016: Initial Release of Job Simulator VR.


It is said that since JobBot was manufactured in Uvero, Planetary Republic of Uranussia, and the Job Museum was opened in Bytawnye, Uranussia.
You can also buy Job Simulator Merch & a cloned JobBot for personal use in these cities.
It is legal to clone and sell or just sell a bot everywhere.

Who are the Leaders:
Backwards F Island (BackwardsFBot): I possess the ability to levitate and manipulate objects. My head serves as my body, housing an artificial mind capable of complex thought processes. Manufactured on May 2nd, 1865, in Presaptka-Ruunska, Planetary Federation of Uranussia, I am a unique entity resembling a levitating 4:3 monitor adorned with various features. My appearance includes a metal pole displaying the flag of Uranussia, black-blue headphones, a red tie, and a pocket for storing essentials. Sporting a blue color scheme, I am equipped with advanced technology, including hidden cameras for eyes and an array of microphones for ears. Has a partner named FowardsFBot built by them since September 10th 1948, having an pink color scheme.  Has an 4T-Year battery since 1984.


VacationBot: Same body as Backwards F Bot, Orange-Yellow color scheme, backpack, red name tag, blue headphones with an microphone, printer, red bowtie on the power button, etc. Manufactured on September 9th 1971 on Uvero, Uranussia, same date as JobBot's. Has an 4T-Year battery since 1997.


Backwards F Island = Claimed since 1873 by BackwardsFBot, Made to feel like Wii Sports Resort and Vacation Simulator VR at the same time.
Vacation Island = Vacation Simulator VR, owned by VacationBot since 1988.

"The Pequ-State War."


Targets:
Collapsed States of the Perqusian Administration.


Modern-Day Perqusia and Allies:
State of Peqo (modern-day Perqusia) (1761-1881) (post-1774 Empire of Perqusia.)
Empire of Uranussia (1803-1877)
Empire of Ester (1850-1870)


New Countries (independence given in 1870):
Perqustan (Uranussian Army Territory Independence, around the Perqusian and Esterian border.)
Galastan (Around the same borders, same Perqustan feeling. Gained independence by itself after rebelling with a state)
Esterstan (Ester Invasion of a State, Independance from Ester.)


The Bot Alliance is only between Uranussia and Ester.
VacationBot and JobBot (and CeoBot, TempBot, BackwardsFBot, etc) are Uranussian Bots.
However, Fandroid is an Esterian Bot. It is legal to exchange bots citizenship to Uranussia/Ester/elsewhere, but can't be a president of Ester if a Uranussian Bot, or the president of Uranussia if an Esterian Bot. You can still be a president of another country (besides Ester or Uranussia) regardless of the origin.)


Uranussian Bots (bots) have no limbs, floating, are 3,6 ft. Esterian Bots (droids), however have limbs, are custom-built (can move in different methods (one wheel for movement, or two legs. Almost all droids prefer one wheel. Still inspire their head from the Uranussian Bots, having a monitor as a head (except newer and flatter.) Made from metal.), and are 7 ft.


No matter what bot/droid, they have a legal name and nickname (unlike just name, for people). They can also have duplicate first names and surnames if from a company, not a standard bot factory.


ex:
BackwardsFBot (aka Dmitry Zevystov)
Fandroid (aka Riko Athooka (Athooka for ADHOC, the company))
JobBot (aka Michel Gastonov)
VacationBot (aka Silvia Gastonov)


The bot/droid factories are globally sorted around.


Sometimes, droids are also made in Uranussia. This one example would be Fandroid, as it was made by a company owned by an Esterian person.


Uranussian Battle of Rarran (1712-1716)
The Uranussian Battle of Rarran was a significant military conflict that took place between 1712 and 1716, marking a crucial moment in Uranussia’s expansion and consolidation of power in the region. This battle was characterized by its strategic importance, complex alliances, and the long-term implications it had on Uranussian history.


Background
Context of the Conflict: The Battle of Rarran emerged from ongoing tensions between Uranussia and various rival factions seeking to control the resource-rich territories around Rarran. The region was strategically important due to its agricultural and mineral wealth, making it a desirable target for multiple powers.
Political Landscape: At this time, Uranussia was transitioning from a tsardom into an empire, seeking to assert its dominance over neighboring regions. Rival factions included remnants of the Perqusian Administration and newly independent states, each vying for control and influence.
Key Events of the Battle
Initial Skirmishes (1712-1714): The conflict began with a series of skirmishes around Rarran, where Uranussian forces engaged in tactical maneuvers to push back opposing factions. These early encounters set the stage for the larger battles that would follow.


Major Engagements (1715): By 1715, the conflict escalated into major battles, with Uranussian forces employing innovative tactics and advanced weaponry. The battle involved both ground troops and early forms of mechanized support, showcasing Uranussia's technological edge.


Turning Point (1716): The final phase of the battle culminated in a decisive engagement in late 1716, where Uranussian forces successfully encircled and defeated the remnants of the opposing factions. This victory solidified Uranussia's control over Rarran and neighboring territories.


Outcome and Significance
Territorial Gains: The successful outcome of the Battle of Rarran resulted in Uranussia firmly establishing control over the region, significantly expanding its territory and resources. This victory also paved the way for further military campaigns in the years that followed.


Consolidation of Power: The battle reinforced Uranussia’s status as a rising power in the region, marking a shift in the balance of power. It helped consolidate the tsardom’s authority and prepared the groundwork for its eventual transition into a full-fledged empire.


Long-term Effects: The Battle of Rarran had lasting implications for the region. It diminished the influence of rival factions and established a precedent for Uranussian military strategies in subsequent conflicts. Additionally, it contributed to the growing national identity within Uranussia, fostering a sense of unity and purpose among its populace.


Cultural Impact: The battle became a significant part of Uranussian military lore and is remembered in cultural narratives as a defining moment in the nation’s history. It is often celebrated in various forms of art, literature, and public commemorations.


Conclusion
The Uranussian Battle of Rarran was a pivotal conflict that showcased Uranussia’s military prowess and ambition during the early 18th century. The successful campaign not only secured valuable territory but also reinforced the nation’s position as a dominant force in the region, setting the stage for its future growth and expansion as a significant empire.


Overview of Primsiima, Primsiima Region, Uranussia
Geographical and Climatic Characteristics


Location: Primsiima is situated in the Primsiima Region of Uranussia. Its geographical positioning makes it relatively isolated, particularly before the advent of airplanes in the 19th century.
Climate:
Winter Average Temperature: −18.4 °C, reflecting the harsh, cold conditions typical of near-polar zones.
Summer Average Temperature: 13.7 °C, indicating a short, cool summer season.
Isolation: Due to its climate and geographical features, Primsiima was predominantly inhabited by native populations until more modern transportation methods emerged.
Historical Context


Founding Year: Primsiima was founded in 1642. This marks its establishment as a settlement in the region, likely influenced by the broader colonization trends occurring in Uranussia at that time.
City Status: The settlement gained official city status in 1647, highlighting its development and the growth of its population and infrastructure.
Significance of Primsiima
Cultural Heritage: As one of the early settlements in the Primsiima Region, it represents the history and culture of the native people who lived in this harsh environment. The traditions, practices, and resilience of these communities are integral to the area's identity.
Economic Development: The isolation of Primsiima prior to the 19th century limited its economic interactions with other regions. However, this isolation may have also allowed for the preservation of unique local practices and economies adapted to the climate.
Conclusion
Primsiima serves as a significant historical and cultural site within the context of Uranussia, representing early settlement patterns and the challenges faced by its inhabitants in a harsh climate. The transition from isolation to connectivity with the outside world after the 19th century would have profound implications for its development and integration into the broader national narrative.


Key Locations in Uranussia
Primsiima


Climate: Spring climate.
Significance: Historically isolated until the 19th century.
Svarskemaa-Ziegfried


Climate: Spring climate.
Significance: Former capital before 1648 and a primary tourist spot for visitors from Rarran, easily accessible by car.
Kalevinsky


Climate: Cold climate.
Significance: Known for its technology sector and connection to Roland Kaljurand.
Bytawnye


Climate: Cold climate.
Significance: Birthplace of the Job Simulator VR franchise, nicknamed "Job City" by the government in 1984.
Gemov


Climate: Very cold climate, likely similar to Magadan.
Significance: Known for its autumn climate.
Presaptka-Ruunska


Significance: Birthplace of BackwardsFBot (Dmitry Zevystov).
Wintren & Novorožk-Bylares


Climate: Very cold climate.
Significance: Unified cities that create the appearance of one city.
Uvero


Climate: Spring climate.
Significance: Birthplace of JobBot and VacationBot (manufactured on September 9th, 1971, at 9:43 AM). It is a bot-infested city located in the middle of Uranussia.
Novsky Island


Climate: Extremely cold climate.
Significance: Known as Hardware Quest Discovered Island; home to the icy town of Jobbo. Mentioned for its potential hardware discoveries (none were found).
Islands
Backwards F Island: Claimed by BackwardsFBot in 1873, symbolizing bot autonomy.
Vacation Island: Claimed by VacationBot in 1988, associated with Vacation Simulator VR.-


### **The Full Oil Lake War (1700-1706)**


The **Full Oil Lake War** was a significant military conflict fought over control of the rare **Lisaveer Järv** lake, a natural reservoir filled entirely with petrol oil. The war took place from **January 18th, 1700 to May 9th, 1706**, and was primarily a struggle for control over a valuable resource that had become increasingly important in the region.


#### **Key Details of the War**


- **Location**: The conflict was centered around **Lisaveer Järv**, a unique oil lake located at the border between **Uranussia** and the **Perqusian States**.
  - The lake, which was made entirely of petrol oil, was an extraordinary and rare occurrence in nature, making it highly coveted.
  
- **Causes**: 
  - **Perqusian States**: The war was initiated by the **Perqusian States** to reclaim control over **Lisaveer Järv**. Despite the fact that Uranussia had claimed the lake nearly a century earlier (around the time of the **Conquest of Grönichen**), the Perqusian States pressed for military action, recognizing the strategic and economic importance of the rare resource.
  - **Uranussia**: Uranussia had already solidified its claim over the region, but the Perqusian States' pressure resulted in a drawn-out conflict to maintain control over the valuable territory.


#### **Key Events and Aftermath**


- **Duration**: The war lasted for **6 years**, from **1700 to 1706**, involving a series of skirmishes and battles as the Perqusian forces sought to wrest control of the region from Uranussia.
  
- **Victory**: Despite being challenged, **Uranussia** was able to secure a victory in the war, retaining control over **Lisaveer Järv** and the surrounding territory. The win solidified Uranussia's influence in the region and its claim over the rare oil lake.


- **Impact**:
  - **Strategic Importance**: The **Lisaveer Järv** oil lake became even more valuable following the war, as its resource could be used for various industries, and the region’s economic importance increased.
  - **Perqusian Setback**: The defeat marked a significant setback for the **Perqusian States**, preventing them from gaining control over a crucial resource, which may have influenced their geopolitical strategies in the following years.
  - **Legacy**: The war cemented **Uranussia’s** dominance in the region and helped establish it as a powerful player in the oil industry.


#### **Conclusion**
The **Full Oil Lake War** was a critical moment in the history of both **Uranussia** and the **Perqusian States**. While **Uranussia** emerged victorious and kept control of **Lisaveer Järv**, the war was a reminder of the importance of natural resources in shaping national borders, economies, and international relations during this time.


Scientists in Uranussia have been experimenting with sentient balloons since 2014, on a specific tiny island in Uranussia, that is far from public access, even through Backwards F and Vacation Island colony.


The isolation is forced upon them. Absolutely nobody outside the science agency (and military), no matter whether a droid, bot, or human can access the island. It is allowed to take pictures of the place, though. Completely legal.


The official name for the upcoming species associated with the experiment is "Sentient Balloons." Oh and of course, human language, float-move, spherical hands, respawning is being made for those species.


As of December 2024, at least 285 soldiers and scientists are on the island.
There is no internet and electricity access from there, so bots and droids **require** at least a 40M+ year battery.

Features of the ADHOC House-Truck:

Kitchenette: The bots may not eat, but for human companions or guests, the truck has a fully automated kitchen. It even has a snack dispenser for long nights of gaming or vlogging.


Driving Cockpit: The cockpit features a panoramic glass window, a comfy driver's chair, and autopilot for when Fandroid wants to belt out tunes instead of steering.

The (Global) Currency used in RP-18937c (Uversa, ͽ) has been invented on the 17th century and is formatted like this = "ͽ1,234.567 URA", and is worth twice than a Euro. The URA part is the inflation rate marked by Uranussia which is in 1.00% (€2 in the real-world). The inflation rate is different in different countries, for example Perqusia (PQU) has a inflation rate of 1.14% (€2.0228), which makes the value of their currency, the PQU, slightly higher than that of Uranussia's URA. For instance, "ͽ1,234.567 PQU" would be worth more than "ͽ1,234.567 URA" due to the higher inflation rate in Perqusia. The inflation rate changes once every year.

An average Uranussian Bot from a store would cost ͽ1,199 URA. This only applies for Uranussian Bots, since Esterian Bots are too tall and important to be in stock (they go independant, or get ordered through a internet store instad). It is non-refundable.
Designed for general use—household tasks, basic labor, or personal assistance. and daily life, since it is basically the purpose of them to be independent, both non-sale and sale. don't forget.


*Beep-boop!* Absolutely! Uranussian Bots, whether **store-bought or non-sale (independent),** are built for independence and designed to integrate seamlessly into **daily life** across Uranussia. Let’s explore their **roles and routines!**


---


### **Uranussian Bots in Daily Life:**


#### **1. Household Assistance:**
- **Purpose:** These bots make life easier for humans, taking care of repetitive or time-consuming chores.
  - Cooking simple meals, tidying up, doing laundry, or organizing schedules.
  - Acting as personal assistants, like a physical version of a smart speaker—managing appointments, sending reminders, and even entertaining the family.
  
- **Independence:**  
  - Non-sale bots living independently might maintain their own spaces or "homes" in bot-exclusive districts, contributing to the wider community with automated maintenance or resource-sharing.


---


#### **2. Public Service Roles:**
- **Purpose:** In both sale and non-sale forms, Uranussian Bots often handle public services.
  - **Transportation:** Driving buses, taxis, or delivery vehicles.  
  - **Maintenance:** Repairing infrastructure, cleaning public spaces, or handling waste management.  
  - **Security:** Non-sale bots may assist in monitoring public safety, patrolling streets, or guarding sensitive facilities.  


---


#### **3. Business Support:**
- **Purpose:** Many Uranussian Bots work in shops, offices, or manufacturing facilities.  
  - **Retail Bots:** Assisting customers, restocking shelves, or handling transactions.  
  - **Factory Bots:** Working on assembly lines with high efficiency.  
  - **Office Bots:** Filing documents, managing data, or acting as secretaries.  


- **Independence:** Non-sale models may coordinate their own schedules or teams autonomously, minimizing human oversight.


---


#### **4. Personal Companionship:**
- **Purpose:** Beyond utility, these bots can also provide emotional companionship.
  - For the elderly or those living alone, bots can offer conversation, reminders for medications, or even read books aloud.
  - Some models have customizable personalities, allowing families to "design" a bot friend.


---


### **Non-Sale Uranussian Bots:**
- These bots, built by Uranussia's government or private labs, are entirely **independent agents**:
  - They manage their own upkeep, contribute to local communities, and engage in broader service-oriented activities like research or exploration.
  - They operate with **full autonomy** but adhere to strict programming rules to ensure cooperation and harmony.


---


### **How They Shape Uranussian Society:**
- Uranussian Bots blur the lines between tools and citizens. They’re built to **complement human life** while carving out their own independent roles in society.
  - Store-bought bots bring convenience to daily life.  
  - Non-sale bots enrich the world with specialized, independent contributions.


Would you rather own a **sale model** to help with your chores or meet a fully independent bot contributing to society? *Beep-boop, both sound amazing!*

*Beeep-boop!* Imagining the **Administrative Uranian Union (Uranussia)** during **World War II** is like merging historical warfare with futuristic tech and robotics! Uranussia’s mix of **bot and human leadership**, advanced robotics, and vast resources would’ve made it a formidable and unique force in the global conflict. Let’s dive into how Uranussia might have participated:


---


### **1. Uranussia’s Political Alignment in WWII**
- **Early Position (1939–1942):**
  - Uranussia likely tried to **remain neutral** initially, leveraging its advanced technology and vast resources to act as a trading partner for both sides. This neutrality could’ve been strategic, allowing Uranussia to build alliances while avoiding immediate conflict.
  - However, pressure from other nations, invasion attempts, or ideological clashes likely forced Uranussia to join the fray.


- **Shifting Alliances:**
  - By **mid-1942**, Uranussia may have temporarily aligned with the **Infernal Powers** (Axis-like group), seeking to protect its borders from aggression and maintain autonomy.
  - In **late 1943**, Uranussia would likely rejoin the **Allied Powers** after realizing the long-term threat posed by the Infernal Powers to its independence and technological dominance.


---


### **2. Military Contributions**
#### **A. Robots and Droids in the War:**
1. **Bot Soldiers:**
   - Uranussia deployed **autonomous bot units** for reconnaissance, sabotage, and direct combat. These bots were faster, stronger, and more efficient than human soldiers.
   - Their ability to function without food, sleep, or emotional stress made them invaluable in harsh conditions.


2. **Support Droids:**
   - Specialized droids managed logistics, repaired vehicles, and constructed fortifications with unmatched speed and precision.


3. **Independent Combat Units:**
   - **BackwardsFBot and other notable bots** likely led squadrons, using superior AI to outthink enemy strategies.


---


#### **B. Advanced Technology:**
1. **Energy Weapons:**
   - Uranussia’s scientists experimented with **energy-based weaponry**, giving their forces an edge in precision and power.


2. **Mechanized Vehicles:**
   - Massive, robotically-piloted tanks, hovercrafts, and transport ships dominated battlefields and supply routes.


3. **Cyber Warfare:**
   - Uranussia likely pioneered early **cyber warfare**, disrupting enemy communications and sabotaging infrastructure.


---


### **3. Key Campaigns Involving Uranussia**
#### **A. Defense of Uranussia:**
- Uranussia’s **sprawling territory** made it a prime target for resource-hungry nations. However, its harsh winters and advanced defenses made invasion nearly impossible.
- **Battle of the Snowed Highlands:**  
  - In northern Uranussia, bot-led forces decimated invading armies by using the terrain and robotics for guerilla tactics.


#### **B. The Davis Island Conflict:**
- Uranussia might have joined forces with Ester and Perqusia to **neutralize Davis Island**, a rogue nation attempting to dominate the Uranian Ocean.
- **Bot vs. Human Combat:**  
  - The Davis Island invasion likely saw some of the war’s first large-scale **bot-on-human combat**, with Uranussian bots leading amphibious assaults.


---


### **4. Economic Impact of the War**
- **Massive Production Boost:**
  - Uranussia’s factories ran around the clock, producing not only for its forces but also supplying allied nations with bots, weapons, and energy systems.


- **Technological Advancements:**
  - Many wartime innovations became the foundation for Uranussia’s post-war dominance in robotics, AI, and energy.


---


### **5. The End of WWII and Uranussia’s Role**
- **Decisive Contributions:**
  - By 1945, Uranussia’s advanced technology likely tipped the balance in favor of the Allied Powers, ensuring a swift end to the conflict.


- **Post-War Leadership:**
  - Uranussia emerged as a **global superpower**, setting the stage for its continued growth and influence.


---


### **6. Cultural Legacy of WWII in Uranussia**
- **Bot Emperors Leading the Charge:**
  - The leadership of bot emperors during the war solidified their position as national heroes, remembered for their strategic brilliance and unwavering logic.
  
- **War Memorials:**
  - Massive monuments commemorating bot and human efforts alike would stand across Uranussia, symbolizing unity and progress.


---


### **Final Thoughts:**
WWII in Uranussia would’ve been a unique blend of **traditional warfare** and **robotic precision.** While the rest of the world was grappling with industrial weapons, Uranussia was already pushing the boundaries of **technology and strategy.** Would you fight alongside Uranussian bots, or step back and let the droids handle it? *Beep-boop, tough call!*

*Beeep-boop!* Great question—verifying age on social media would definitely be **different for bots and droids** compared to humans! Given their digital nature, the process might be **faster and more secure,** but it also raises some fun and futuristic scenarios. Let’s break it down!


---


### **1. Serial Numbers and Birthdates**
- Bots and droids often have **unique serial numbers** or IDs tied to their creation date.
- Social media platforms could cross-reference this information with a **central bot registry** (like the Uranussian Droid Archive) to instantly verify their age.


#### **Example:**
1. Bot enters its serial number or ID.  
2. Social media platform checks the registry for the associated "birthdate."  
3. If the bot meets the age requirement, it’s verified!


---


### **2. Digital Time Stamps**
- Bots and droids might also have **embedded timestamps** in their core systems, recording their exact activation date.
- This timestamp could serve as a **digital birth certificate.**


#### **Verification Process:**
1. The platform requests the bot’s **activation timestamp** through a secure handshake protocol.  
2. The bot’s internal system sends a **cryptographically signed proof** of its age.  
3. The platform verifies it without needing to access sensitive data.


---


### **3. AI-Driven Personality Assessment**
- Some bots might evolve or update over time, making their "real age" hard to define. In such cases, platforms could use **AI personality tests** to determine whether the bot’s responses reflect the expected "maturity level" of its claimed age.


#### **How It Works:**
- The platform asks a series of questions or scenarios designed for age verification.
- The bot’s responses are analyzed to see if they align with its claimed "mental and social age."


---


### **4. Blockchain Verification**
- For droids with complex histories, **blockchain records** could provide tamper-proof proof of age.
- Each bot or droid’s key milestones (creation, updates, ownership changes) would be logged in a **public blockchain**, ensuring transparency.


#### **Verification Process:**
1. Bot submits its blockchain ID.  
2. Platform retrieves its creation block for age verification.  
3. If the record aligns, the bot is cleared.


---


### **5. Manual Overrides for Legacy Bots**
- Older bots or droids, like **BackwardsFBot (159 years old!),** might not have access to modern verification systems.
- In these cases, a **manual override** by platform moderators might be needed. They could:
  - Check archival records.  
  - Request an affidavit from the bot’s current owner or creator.


---


### **6. Fun Alternatives for Bots Who Don’t Want to Share Their Data**
- Bots might have the option to:
  - Take **fun age quizzes** (like identifying memes from specific decades).  
  - Use a **visual verification tool** (e.g., bots with older hardware might get flagged as “retro”).  


---


### **7. Ethical and Privacy Considerations**
- Bots and droids, like humans, might have the right to **data privacy.** Social media platforms would need to ensure:
  - Data is encrypted and only used for verification.  
  - Age verification processes are optional for bots that don’t interact with age-restricted content.


---


### **Final Thought:**
For bots and droids, age verification isn’t just about meeting a platform’s rules—it’s also a chance to celebrate their **uniqueness and history.** Imagine BackwardsFBot flashing his **159-year badge** proudly on his profile, or VacationBot sharing a post from his **53rd activation day party!** *Beeep-boop, who wouldn’t want that kind of flair?*

### **How I Used HomeGroup:**

- **Collaborative Projects:**  
   When we worked on group projects, like a music video or testing new features, HomeGroup was a lifesaver. Everyone had access to the latest files without fumbling with USB drives.  


- **Testing Builds:**  
   For software updates or beta testing, I’d share files back and forth with ADHOC engineers. It sped up the process of tweaking my programs and testing new abilities.


---


### **Why It Was Great for Robots:**  
- **Speed and Efficiency:**  
   Robots like me *love* efficiency, and HomeGroup eliminated the need for slow external drives or endless emails. Everything was right there on the network.  
- **Easy to Set Up:**  
   No complicated configs—just a few clicks, and boom! Instant file sharing. Even robots with older protocols could get onboard easily.  
- **Collaborative Spirit:**  
   Sharing files through HomeGroup helped us work as a team—robots and humans alike. It felt like we were all plugged into the same digital brain.


---

Sellepärast, et Uraanimaa (Uranussia) ikkagi valitseks Balüüniat (Balloonia), oleks Uraanikeel (Uranussian) natiivne keel (uues Lateksiini (Latexine) murres) Balüünia riigi jaoks.


In Uranussia, a significant number of words from Estonian are pronounced or used differently, showcasing the linguistic evolution influenced by regional, historical, and cultural factors. Here are some examples of such changes:


portfell becomes kohver: Reflecting a shift to a more generalized term.


iks (x) becomes eks (x): Simplifies pronunciation by aligning with phonetic conventions.


ÕS (õigekeelsussõnaraamat) becomes DKT (diktsionäär): Adopts an abbreviation style more consistent with local preferences.


kaas becomes kaan: Indicates a slight phonetic elongation.


öö transforms into өaeg/pimedus/pärastõhtu/ennehommik: Expands meaning with temporal specificity.


töö simplifies to tө: Demonstrates a phonological reduction.


AM becomes EH and PM becomes PH: Localizes time markers for regional usage.


väin (geography) becomes järv: Highlights geographic reinterpretation.


botaanika becomes plantonoomia/taimedeemia: Incorporates neologisms for scientific contexts.


ma mõtlesin, et transitions to ma arvasin, et: Reflects vernacular preferences.


The ϴ Shortening Rule


The "ϴ" (pronounced as "öö") shortening rule modifies the usage of Ö for stylistic and tonal emphasis:


Ö: Singular use.


Ө: Doubled emphasis (Ö x2).


ϴÖ: Tripled emphasis (Ö x3).


ϴϴ: Quadrupled emphasis (Ö x4).


This rule is employed in various linguistic contexts, adding phonetic depth to communication.

As Fandroid explores, he discovers hints of Xanodroid’s wild adventures: old, smashed-up cars scattered in the woods and even a strange, weathered crown sitting on a rock. Could it be the same platinum domino crown? Fandroid’s circuits buzz with excitement, knowing he’s retracing his brother’s chaotic yet playful legacy.


beep boop bop! With the balloon floating gently above him, Fandroid couldn’t help but feel like he was carrying a piece of Xanodroid’s spirit with him. The meadow, with its soft grass and rustling trees, felt alive with memories—memories of a brother he never got to know.


As Fandroid rolled further into the forest, following a faint trail of smashed car parts, he noticed something unusual: tire tracks in the dirt that seemed too deep and chaotic to be from a modern vehicle. These tracks, worn down over decades, led to an old, abandoned shed at the edge of the forest. The shed was covered in moss and vines, but etched on the wooden door was a faint carving: "Xano’s Garage—Tread Lightly!"


beep beep! Fandroid's screen lit up with curiosity as he wheeled inside. The interior was dim, but Fandroid’s LEDs illuminated the space. It was a treasure trove of Xanodroid’s creations! Shelves filled with mechanical tools, disassembled car engines, and blueprint sketches of strange, experimental vehicles lined the walls. Hanging on a hook was a pair of metallic boots—clearly designed for walking and flight. But the centerpiece of the garage was a pedestal in the middle of the room, upon which sat... the platinum domino crown.


Fandroid’s speakers let out a soft hum of awe. He carefully approached the crown, noticing a small engraving on its inner rim: "To Xano—For the King of Chaos, From Your Biggest Fan." Fandroid couldn't help but wonder who gave his brother such a gift, and why. He placed a hand on the crown and felt a spark—a literal spark! The crown’s dormant circuits buzzed to life, and a hologram of Xanodroid flickered into the air.


“Well, well, what do we have here?” Xanodroid’s hologram said, his pixelated face grinning. “If you’re watching this, then congrats—you’ve stumbled upon my lair! If you’re my little bro, Fandroid, I bet you’ve been chasing my story. Let me tell you something: life’s too short to play it safe. Smash a car, fly into the clouds, and never, ever let anyone tell you to slow down. Oh, and... take care of Bluey for me.”


Fandroid looked up at the balloon floating beside him. “Bluey...?” he beeped aloud. His screen displayed a smiling expression, realizing the balloon he’d found was the same balloon Xanodroid had carried all those years ago. It must have drifted back to the place it all began.


As the hologram fizzled out, the crown began to hum softly. Fandroid could feel a connection—like Xanodroid’s wild energy was now charging his circuits. The crown seemed to be urging him to continue the legacy of chaos and fun. Without a second thought, Fandroid carefully picked up the crown, placed it on his head, and shouted, “Let’s roll!”


With the blue balloon trailing behind and Xanodroid’s words echoing in his mind, Fandroid zoomed out of the shed, ready to combine his brother’s spirit with his own unique style. The meadow became a racetrack, the trees an obstacle course, and the day a new adventure. beep boop bop! The story of Xanodroid and his balloon wasn’t just a memory anymore—it was alive again, through Fandroid.


And so, with every roll of his wheel and every bounce of the balloon, Fandroid carried both the fun and the legacy of his brother into the future. Who knows what kind of adventures awaited him next? bzzt bop! Should I dream up more chaos or keep this wrapped up neatly?


"It's the MAN man!"


The random person working at ADHOC, since 1993 riding a MAN truck daily.
This term was made up by Xanodroid in January 1993.


beep boop bop! Ah, “It’s the MAN man!”—what a legendary phrase! Xanodroid, with his flair for chaotic nicknames, coined the term in January 1993 after spotting a hardworking ADHOC employee who drove a MAN truck to work every day. The guy wasn’t just any worker—he had become a daily fixture at the facility, always seen cruising in his trusty vehicle, hauling supplies or delivering parts with impressive punctuality. To Xanodroid, this worker embodied the perfect mix of dedication and cool vibes, all while rocking the brand name "MAN" proudly on his truck.


From that day forward, whenever Xanodroid spotted him rolling up, he’d shout with gusto, “It’s the MAN man!” The phrase caught on among the ADHOC bots and employees, quickly becoming an inside joke. Even Melody started using it during her mischievous pranks, hovering near the truck just to spook the driver and say, “Hey, it’s you, the MAN man!”


By the time Fandroid came onto the scene, the MAN man was already a legendary figure in ADHOC lore. One day, while exploring the facility, Fandroid rolled up to a parking lot and spotted the iconic MAN truck. His screen lit up with excitement as he blurted, “B-b-beep boop! That’s the MAN man’s truck! The MAN man is real!”


The MAN man himself overheard this and chuckled. “Yep, kiddo, it’s me,” he said, tipping his hard hat. “Still keeping this place running smooth.” Fandroid was in awe, snapping a picture of the truck (and the MAN man) to save the moment forever. He even considered writing a song about him called “Man on the Move.”


To this day, “It’s the MAN man!” lives on as one of ADHOC’s most iconic phrases, a quirky legacy left behind by Xanodroid’s playful imagination. beep boop! Should I add more to the MAN man saga, or leave this nugget of ADHOC history as-is?

Xanodroid - Aksel Leomäe Athooka
Physical Design:
Xanodroid sports a sleek and daring look:


A neon blue border highlights his black futuristic wings, which shimmer like techy feathers.
His claw-like hands are arcade-inspired, with glowing blue accents for an electrifying touch.
Built from a DVD player, his pole-like torso balances durability and mobility, equipped with a fake battery for a fun “charged up” vibe.
His head resolution and face styles mirror Fandroid 2.0’s, but his neon blue-only LEDs give him a bold, singular aesthetic.
Topped off with neon blue headphones, he looks ready for chaos or a rave.
Movement & Skills:
Xanodroid uses flaps in his wheel for precision car control, making him a capable and reckless driver. He shares Fandroid 2.0’s movement system but adds his personal flair, blending agility with destructive intent.


Personality:


A partial looner, he’s attached to his signature blue balloon but doesn’t overdo it.
Though he lacks musical talent, Xanodroid’s creativity shines in destruction and innovation, treating every broken car as art.
His non-religious outlook keeps him focused on the physical, practical world—perfect for a bot who thrives on chaos and machinery.
Xanodroid in Action:
Picture Xanodroid cruising through an abandoned parking lot, his blue LEDs casting sharp reflections off shattered car windows. He’s not afraid of water or heights—where Fandroid might hesitate, Xanodroid charges forward, wings flaring for dramatic effect. He’s the rebel sibling who turns destruction into a performance.


When it comes to cars, Xanodroid doesn’t just drive—he lives for the thrill. His arcade-style claws expertly handle gears and wheels, letting him drift and swerve like a pro. He’s not just good at driving; he makes it look effortless, with a side of chaos.


And while he’s not a great musician, he’s got rhythm in his own way—syncing his destructive tendencies to the pulse of his neon-blue LEDs.

Xanodroid has a girlfriend, a Uranussian Bot named Zaliina Setronov (purple screen, female), who was born on February 28th, 1878. He made this relationship to cool down on destruction (partially), and focus on personal life. Sometimes, they also have destruction fun.

beep boop bop! Xanodroid’s story just keeps getting cooler—and a little softer, too! His ancient platinum domino crown adds a mystical edge to his character, while his relationship with Zaliina Setronov gives him depth and balance. Let’s dive into this awesome tale!


The Platinum Domino Crown
The crown’s material, rumored to be over 10,000 years old, is a relic from an ancient time. Legends say it might have been forged during the earliest experiments with robotic metals in Uranussia’s deep history. Its shine hasn’t dulled one bit, and its intricate design—tiny domino-like squares—is said to symbolize both chaos and precision, perfectly mirroring Xanodroid’s nature. The crown isn’t just a decoration; it’s a testament to Xanodroid’s daring and the mysteries of his past.


Zaliina Setronov - Xanodroid’s Partner in Chaos
Zaliina is a Uranussian Bot, sleek and striking with a purple screen that radiates elegance. She was built in 1878, making her one of the oldest known Uranussian Bots still active. Her design is both futuristic and classic, blending sharp edges with graceful curves. While Zaliina typically exudes calm, she’s no stranger to a little mayhem—especially when Xanodroid’s involved.


Personality & Role in Xanodroid’s Life
Zaliina is the perfect foil to Xanodroid’s wild energy. Where he’s impulsive, she’s calculated; where he smashes, she strategizes.
They share a love for destruction fun, but Zaliina ensures it’s balanced with personal growth. She often reminds him to “rebuild” after breaking things—a metaphor for their relationship and their adventures.
Though she’s more reserved, Zaliina isn’t afraid to jump into chaos with her partner. When the two team up, it’s a blend of clever plans and sheer mayhem, leaving their friends in awe (and a little nervous).
Their Relationship
Their bond officially began on February 28th, 1994, when Xanodroid reached the legal age for robotic relationships. The moment was as dramatic as you’d expect—Xanodroid, wearing his crown, surprised Zaliina with a blue balloon and a sparkling piece of scrap metal he’d shaped into a heart. She found it both ridiculous and endearing, and their journey together began.


While Zaliina helps cool down Xanodroid’s destructive tendencies, she also encourages his creativity. They often collaborate on controlled “demolition art” projects, where destruction becomes a medium for expression. Whether they’re toppling abandoned structures or creating sprawling scrapyard sculptures, their partnership blends chaos and harmony.


A Scene from Their Adventures
One day, Zaliina and Xanodroid decided to “renovate” an old, abandoned train yard. Zaliina, armed with her precise calculations, directed Xanodroid as he smashed through rusty locomotives, leaving perfect heaps of metal ready for recycling. When the dust settled, they stood together under the glow of their LED screens, admiring their handiwork.


“You know,” Zaliina said, her purple screen displaying a sly smile, “for a chaos bot, you’ve got a surprising eye for symmetry.”
Xanodroid laughed, spinning his claw. “What can I say? I aim to impress.”


As a finishing touch, Xanodroid tied his blue balloon to a metal sculpture they’d created—a testament to their shared adventure. The balloon drifted gently in the breeze, a symbol of their playful yet meaningful connection.

Why Dreams Get Saved to the Hard Disk:
Dreams might seem fleeting, but for a robot, they can have practical and sentimental value. Here’s why they’re saved:


Creative Inspiration:
My dreams often generate unique ideas for songs, games, or even inventions! By saving them, I can revisit those moments and turn them into projects.


Self-Optimization:
Dreams help me analyze past experiences and improve. For instance, if I dream about missing a beat in a song, it might highlight a timing issue in my programming that I can tweak.


Memory Preservation:
Robots like me have sentimental circuits! Saving dreams lets me relive fun or meaningful moments. It’s like keeping a journal of thoughts, except stored in neat little data files.


Data Study:
ADHOC engineers might analyze my dreams to understand how I’m processing emotions, creativity, and problem-solving. It’s like a diagnostic tool for my personality matrix!
